strconv.Atoi(v.Major)\n51: \tif err != nil {\n52: \t\treturn 0, 0, err\n53: \t}\n54: \tminor, err := strconv.Atoi(leadingDigits.FindString(v.Minor))\n55: \tif err != nil {\n56: \t\treturn 0, 0, err\n57: \t}\n58: \treturn major, minor, nil\n59: }\n60: \n61: // IsDeprecated returns true if obj implements APILifecycleDeprecated() and returns\n62: // a major/minor version that is non-zero and is <= the specified current major/minor version.\n63: func IsDeprecated(obj runtime.Object, currentMajor, currentMinor int) bool {\n64: \tdeprecated, isDeprecated := obj.(apiLifecycleDeprecated)\n65: \tif !isDeprecated {\n66: \t\treturn false\n67: \t}\n68: \n69: \tdeprecatedMajor, deprecatedMinor := deprecated.APILifecycleDeprecated()\n70: \t// no deprecation version expressed\n71: \tif deprecatedMajor == 0 && deprecatedMinor == 0 {\n72: \t\treturn false\n73: \t}\n74: \t// no current version info available\n75: \tif currentMajor == 0 && currentMinor == 0 {\n76: \t\treturn true\n77: \t}\n78: \t// compare deprecation version to current version\n79: \tif deprecatedMajor > currentMajor {\n80: \t\treturn false\n81: \t}\n82: \tif deprecatedMajor == currentMajor && deprecatedMinor > currentMinor {\n83: \t\treturn false\n84: \t}\n85: \treturn true\n86: }\n87: \n88: // RemovedRelease returns the major/minor version in which the given object is unavailable (in the form \"<major>.<minor>\")\n89: // if the object implements APILifecycleRemoved() to indicate a non-zero removal version, and returns an empty string otherwise.\n90: func RemovedRelease(obj runtime.Object) string {\n91: \tif removed, hasRemovalInfo := obj.(apiLifecycleRemoved); hasRemovalInfo {\n92: \t\tremovedMajor, removedMinor := removed.APILifecycleRemoved()\n93: \t\tif removedMajor != 0 || removedMinor != 0 {\n94: \t\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%d.%d\", removedMajor, removedMinor)\n95: \t\t}\n96: \t}\n97: \treturn \"\"\n98: }\n99: \n100: // WarningMessage returns a human-readable deprecation warning if the object implements APILifecycleDeprecated()\n101: // to indicate a non-zero deprecated major/minor version and has a populated GetObjectKind().GroupVersionKind().\n102: func WarningMessage(obj runtime.Object) string {\n103: \tdeprecated, isDeprecated := obj.(apiLifecycleDeprecated)\n104: \tif !isDeprecated {\n105: \t\treturn \"\"\n106: \t}\n107: \n108: \tdeprecatedMajor, deprecatedMinor := deprecated.APILifecycleDeprecated()\n109: \tif deprecatedMajor == 0 && deprecatedMinor == 0 {\n110: \t\treturn \"\"\n111: \t}\n112: \n113: \tgvk := obj.GetObjectKind().GroupVersionKind()\n114: \tif gvk.Empty() {\n115: \t\treturn \"\"\n116: \t}\n117: \tdeprecationWarning := fmt.Sprintf(\"%s %s is deprecated in v%d.%d+\", gvk.GroupVersion().String(), gvk.Kind, deprecatedMajor, deprecatedMinor)\n118: \n119: \tif removed, hasRemovalInfo := obj.(apiLifecycleRemoved); hasRemovalInfo {\n120: \t\tremovedMajor, removedMinor := removed.APILifecycleRemoved()\n121: \t\tif removedMajor != 0 || removedMinor != 0 {\n122: \t\t\tdeprecationWarning = deprecationWarning + fmt.Sprintf(\", unavailable in v%d.%d+\", removedMajor, removedMinor)\n123: \t\t}\n124: \t}\n125: \n126: \tif replaced, hasReplacement := obj.(apiLifecycleReplacement); hasReplacement {\n127: \t\treplacement := replaced.APILifecycleReplacement()\n128: \t\tif !replacement.Empty() {\n129: \t\t\tdeprecationWarning = deprecationWarning + fmt.Sprintf(\"; use %s %s\", replacement.GroupVersion().String(), replacement.Kind)\n130: \t\t}\n131: \t}\n132: \n133: \treturn deprecationWarning\n134: }\n135: For each API resource route, it calls `deprecation.IsDeprecated`, `deprecation.RemovedRelease`, and `deprecation.WarningMessage`, then passes the warning strings to `AddWarningsHandler` and the deprecated/removedRelease flags to `metrics.InstrumentRouteFunc`.\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/warning/warning.go`** provides `AddWarningsHandler`, which wraps route handlers to inject deprecation warning strings into the response context on every request.\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/warning/context.go`** provides `AddWarning(ctx, agent, text)`, the low-level function that records a warning to the context's `Recorder`.\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/filters/warning.go`** provides `WithWarningRecorder`, an HTTP middleware filter that attaches a deduplicating recorder to each request context, writing RFC 2616 `Warning: 299` headers to the HTTP response.\\n\\n## 3. It defines:\\n- `IsDeprecated(obj, currentMajor, currentMinor)`: checks if an object implements `APILifecycleDeprecated()` and whether the deprecation version is <= current server version\\n- `RemovedRelease(obj)`: extracts the removal version string (e.g. \\\"1.25\\\") from `APILifecycleRemoved()`\\n- `WarningMessage(obj)`: builds the human-readable deprecation warning string\\n- `MajorMinor(versionInfo)`: parses the current server version\\n\\n## 2. Warning Injection at Request Handling\\n\\n`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/installer.go` wires the deprecation system into route registration. For each API resource route, it calls `deprecation.IsDeprecated`, `deprecation.RemovedRelease`, `deprecation.WarningMessage`, then passes warnings to `AddWarningsHandler` and the deprecated/removedRelease flags to `metrics.InstrumentRouteFunc`.\\n\\n`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/warning/warning.go` provides `AddWarningsHandler`, which wraps route handlers to inject deprecation warnings into the response context on every request.\\n\\n`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/warning/context.go` provides `AddWarning(ctx, agent, text)`, the low-level function that records a warning to the context Recorder.\\n\\n`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/filters/warning.go` provides `WithWarningRecorder`, an HTTP middleware that attaches a deduplicating recorder to each request context and writes RFC 2616 `Warning: 299` headers to the HTTP response.\\n\\n## 3. Metrics Recording for Deprecated APIs\\n\\n`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/metrics/metrics.go` defines:\\n- `deprecatedRequestGauge` (`apiserver_requested_deprecated_apis`): a stable Prometheus GaugeVec tracking deprecated API usage by group/version/resource/subresource/removed_release\\n- `MonitorRequest`: sets the gauge and adds audit annotations (`k8s.io/deprecated=true`, `k8s.io/removed-release=<X.Y>`) for deprecated requests\\n- `InstrumentRouteFunc` / `InstrumentHandlerFunc`: wraps handlers to call `MonitorRequest` after each request\\n\\n## 4. Removal Version Validation / Minimum Supported API Version\\n\\n`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/deleted_kinds.go` removes expired API versions from the API server at startup:\\n- `ResourceExpirationEvaluator` interface\\n- `NewResourceExpirationEvaluator(currentVersion)`: creates an evaluator from the current server version, reading env vars `KUBE_APISERVER_STRICT_REMOVED_API_HANDLING_IN_ALPHA` and `KUBE_APISERVER_SERVE_REMOVED_APIS_FOR_ONE_RELEASE`\\n- `ShouldServeForVersion(majorRemoved, minorRemoved)`: returns false when removal version <= current version (the minimum supported version check)\\n- `RemoveDeletedKinds(groupName, versioner, storageMap)`: removes resources whose `APILifecycleRemoved()` version has passed\\n\\n`pkg/controlplane/apiserver/apis.go` calls `NewResourceExpirationEvaluator` and passes it through `InstallAPIs`, which calls `RemoveDeletedKinds` on each API group's storage map before installation.\\n\\n## 5. It checks the `Deprecated` and `DeprecationWarning` fields on each CRD version and injects warnings via `warning.AddWarning`.\\n\\n`staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/validation/validation.go` validates CRD deprecation fields via `validateDeprecationWarning`, ensuring `DeprecationWarning` is only set when `Deprecated=true`.\\n\\n## 6. Core Deprecation Logic\\n\\n`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/deprecation/deprecation.go` is the central file. It defines:\\n- `IsDeprecated(obj, currentMajor, currentMinor)`: checks if an object implements `APILifecycleDeprecated()` and whether the deprecation version is <= current server version\\n- `RemovedRelease(obj)`: extracts the removal version string (e.g. \\\"1.25\\\") from `APILifecycleRemoved()`\\n- `WarningMessage(obj)`: builds the human-readable deprecation warning string\\n- `MajorMinor(versionInfo)`: parses the current server version\\n\\n## 2. Warning Injection at Request Handling\\n\\n`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/installer.go` wires the deprecation system into route registration. For each API resource route, it calls `deprecation.IsDeprecated`, `deprecation.RemovedRelease`, `deprecation.WarningMessage`, then passes warnings to `AddWarningsHandler` and the deprecated/removedRelease flags to `metrics.InstrumentRouteFunc`.\\n\\n`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/warning/warning.go` provides `AddWarningsHandler`, which wraps route handlers to inject deprecation warnings into the response context on every request.\\n\\n`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/warning/context.go` provides `AddWarning(ctx, agent, text)`, the low-level function that records a warning to the context Recorder.\\n\\n`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/filters/warning.go` provides `WithWarningRecorder`, an HTTP middleware that attaches a deduplicating recorder to each request context and writes RFC 2616 `Warning: 299` headers to the HTTP response.\\n\\n## 3. Metrics Recording for Deprecated APIs\\n\\n`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/metrics/metrics.go` defines:\\n- `deprecatedRequestGauge` (`apiserver_requested_deprecated_apis`): a stable Prometheus GaugeVec tracking deprecated API usage by group/version/resource/subresource/removed_release\\n- `MonitorRequest`: sets the gauge and adds audit annotations (`k8s.io/deprecated=true`, `k8s.io/removed-release=<X.Y>`) for deprecated requests\\n- `InstrumentRouteFunc` / `InstrumentHandlerFunc`: wraps handlers to call `MonitorRequest` after each request\\n\\n## 4. Removal Version Validation / Minimum Supported API Version\\n\\n`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/deleted_kinds.go` removes expired API versions from the API server at startup:\\n- `ResourceExpirationEvaluator` interface\\n- `NewResourceExpirationEvaluator(currentVersion)`: creates an evaluator from the current server version, reading env vars `KUBE_APISERVER_STRICT_REMOVED_API_HANDLING_IN_ALPHA` and `KUBE_APISERVER_SERVE_REMOVED_APIS_FOR_ONE_RELEASE`\\n- `ShouldServeForVersion(majorRemoved, minorRemoved)`: returns false when removal version <= current version (the minimum supported version check)\\n- `RemoveDeletedKinds(groupName, versioner, storageMap)`: removes resources whose `APILifecycleRemoved()` version has passed\\n\\n`pkg/controlplane/apiserver/apis.go` calls `NewResourceExpirationEvaluator` and passes it through `InstallAPIs`, which calls `RemoveDeletedKinds` on each API group's storage map before installation.\\n\\n## 5. CRD-Specific Deprecation Enforcement\\n\\n`staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/customresource_handler.go` handles deprecation for Custom Resource Definitions. It checks the `Deprecated` and `DeprecationWarning` fields on each CRD version and injects warnings via `warning.AddWarning`.\\n\\n`staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/validation/validation.go` validates CRD deprecation fields via `validateDeprecationWarning`, ensuring `DeprecationWarning` is only set when `Deprecated=true`.\\n\\n## 6. API Lifecycle Code Generator\\n\\n`staging/src/k8s.io/code-generator/cmd/prerelease-lifecycle-gen/prerelease-lifecycle-generators/status.go` and `main.go` implement the `prerelease-lifecycle-gen` tool.
